            (function($) {
                var timer;
                $("#edition_nav, #region_nav").click(function() {
                    $(this).toggleClass("edition_nav_selected");
                }).mouseleave(function(){
                    var e = $(this);
                    timer && clearTimeout(timer);
                    timer = setTimeout(function(){
                        e.hasClass('edition_nav_selected') && e.removeClass('edition_nav_selected')
                    }, 1000);
                }).mouseenter(function(){
                timer && clearTimeout(timer);
                });

																										<div class="articleBody" itemprop="articleBody">
								
																		
                                    
									<p>DETROIT -- Nissan is lowering the price of its Leaf electric car to try to boost anemic sales.</p>

<p>The 2013 Leaf will start at $28,800, which is $6,000 lower than the previous model, company executives said Monday at the Detroit auto show. When combined with the federal electric-vehicle tax credit of $7,500 and other state and local tax incentives, the price could fall as low as $18,800 in California. That would make it comparable to gas-powered and hybrid cars of its size like the Toyota Prius. It would also be far lower than the electric Ford Focus or Chevrolet Volt, which both start around $39,000.</p>
									
									<p>The 2013 Leaf goes on sale in February.</p>

<p>General Motors North American President Mark Reuss said he doesn't expect his company to match Nissan's price cut on the Volt.</p>

<p>"It's a different car, we all know that," he said Monday in an interview. "It's got a different battery and it's got a different range."</p>

<p>The Volt can go about 35 miles on battery power before a gas-powered generator kicks in to run the car. The Leaf can go about 73 miles per charge, but its lithium-ion batteries must be recharged to go farther than that.</p>

<p>Reuss said at that price, Nissan will post big losses on the Leaf. But he said the company needs the sales because it has to keep its new battery and assembly plants in Tennessee running.</p>

<p>"They're firing up a plant. They've got to sell a plant" worth of cars, he said.</p>

<p>The Leaf has consistently missed Nissan's sales goals since it went on sale at the end of 2010. Nissan CEO Carlos Ghosn said he hoped Leaf sales would jump 50 percent last year after the company expanded the number of dealerships offering them. But worldwide sales rose just 22 percent to around 27,000. U.S. Leaf sales were up just 1.5 percent to less than 10,000.</p>

	<div id="ad_mid_article" class="ad_wrapper"><script type="text/javascript">
HPAds.adSonar(1523709,2259768,300,250);
</script></div><p>Nissan CEO Carlos Ghosn said the lower price should help attract more customers. Ghosn didn't say whether Nissan will lose money on the Leaf, but he said the company is spending less on some parts in the 2013 model. It also cut manufacturing costs when it moved production of Leafs for the U.S. market from Japan to Tennessee.</p>

<p>Ghosn said the lack of recharging infrastructure is hurting electric car sales, since potential buyers are worried about the cars running out of power while they're driving.</p>

<p>Nissan is lobbying for the development of public charging stations, but Ghosn called that "a long-term battle." He was clearly frustrated that some governments &ndash; like those in Japan and France &ndash; are promoting and funding electric vehicle infrastructure more than others.</p>

<p>"We have everything ready. The cars are ready. The technology is ready," he said.</p>

<p>Despite those frustrations, Ghosn said, Nissan won't abandon electric technology, and he still believes electric cars could make up 10 percent of Nissan's sales by 2020.</p>

<p>"Zero emissions are here to stay, and we think this is going to be an important part of the industry," he said.</p>

<p>___</p>

<p>Auto Writer Tom Krisher contributed to this report from Detroit.</p>

						var previous_slideshow_obj		= document.slideshow_models[previous_slideshow_id];
			var previous_slideshow_wrapper	= previous_slideshow_obj.dom.$wrapper;
			var screen_mode					= null;

			post_slideshow_callback = function(slideshow_model) 
			{
				if ( !slideshow_model.dom.$mainWrapper.length )
					return;

				document.slideshow_models[slideshow_id] = slideshow_model;	

				huff && huff.use('modal', function(m){
					m.hide();
				});
	
				// Important: Don't remove the following if else or sequence of event calls
				// these reset and correct the sizing of the inline ajax loaded slideshow  
				if ( 'fullscreen' === screen_mode 
					&& 'fixed' === previous_slideshow_obj.dom.$wrapper.css('position') ) {

					previous_slideshow_obj.exitFullscreen();
					slideshow_model.enterFullscreen();
					slideshow_model.exitFullscreen();
					slideshow_model.enterFullscreen();
				} else {
					slideshow_model.enterFullscreen();
					slideshow_model.exitFullscreen();
				}

				$('.hp-slideshow-wrapper-mask').remove();
				$('.hp-remove-ss-element').remove();
				previous_slideshow_obj.dom.$mainWrapper.remove();
				delete(document.slideshow_models[previous_slideshow_id]);

				$wrapper.show();
				
				// To highlight the new slideshow
				slideshow_model.expandPane();

				// Fullscreen only slideshow
				if ( 1 === slideshow_model.activeSlideshow().fullscreen_only ) {
					jQuery('.hp-ss-fs-teaser').click();
				}
				
				try {
					var slide_top_pos = slideshow_model.dom.$mainWrapper.position().top || false;
					if ( slide_top_pos ) {
						jQuery("body").animate( { scrollTop: slide_top_pos + "px" } );
					}
				} catch(e) {
				}
				
				return;
			};
		}
		
		var ready = function() 
		{
			if ( loaded ) {
				return;
			}
			loaded = true;
			
			var modules, requests = 2;
						
			var render = function() {
								$wrapper.removeClass('hp-slideshow-wrapper-loading').slideshow( {
					modules : modules,
					include : ['css','slides','inline','arrows','thumbs','expand_base','leaderboard','expand_details','fullscreen','timer','tracking','touch','data_beacon']				}, post_slideshow_callback);
			};
			
							
				if ( true === ajax_loaded )
				{
									}
				else
				{
					var params = {};
					
					
					if (!params || params instanceof Array) 
						params = { };

					params.v = 1;
					params._id_slideshow = '274592';
					params.entry_id = '2478185';
					$.ajax({ type : 'GET', url : '/_slideshows/published.php', data : params, success : function( data ) {
						$( '#slideshow_json_e457251f9b17cd0605afabbc49abecad' ).data( 'slideshow', data );
						if ( --requests <= 0 ) render();
					} });
				}
			
						
			require.config( { 
				baseUrl : 'http://s.huffpost.com/assets/js.php?f=',
				paths   : { 'slideshows' : '_slideshows/modules', 'slideshow_styles' : '_slideshows/modules' }
			} );
			require( ['http://s.huffpost.com/assets/js.php?f=jquery%2Fui%2Fjquery.ui.mouse.min.js%2Cjquery%2Fui%2Fjquery.ui.draggable.min.js%2Cjquery%2Fplugins%2Fjquery.easing.1.3.js%2Cjquery%2Fplugins%2Fjquery.mousewheel.min.js&v=1377630675','http://s.huffpost.com/assets/js.php?f=jquery%2Fplugins%2Fjquery.scrollbar.js&v=1377630675'], function() {
				
				var version = '';
				if ( window.huff 
						&& 'object' === typeof huff.versions 
						&& huff.versions.deploy_seq ) {
					version = huff.versions.deploy_seq;
				}

				require.config( { urlArgs : 'v=' + version } );

				require( [ 'slideshows/min/slideshowcore.built.min' ], function() {
					modules = arguments.length > 1 ? Array.prototype.slice.call( arguments, 1 ) : [ ];
					if ( --requests <= 0 ) render();
				} );
				require.config( { urlArgs : '' } );
			} );
		};
		
		var windowScroll = function() {
			if ( $window.scrollTop() + $window.height() > $wrapper.offset().top ){
				$window.unbind( 'scroll', windowScroll );
				ready();
				return true;
			}
		};
		var match = location.hash.match( /slide=[^&]*/i ), sid = 0, target;
		if ( match != null && match[0].split( 'slide=' )[1].match( /\d+/ ) ) {
			ready();
		}
		else if (!windowScroll()) {
			$window.bind( 'scroll', windowScroll );
		}
	});
}(jQuery));
</script>

<script type="text/javascript"> var src_url="https://spshared.5min.com/Scripts/PlayerSeed.js?playList=517550208&height=411&width=570&sid=577&origin=SOLR&relatedMode=2&relatedBottomHeight=60&companionPos=&hasCompanion=false&autoStart=false&colorPallet=%23FFEB00&videoControlDisplayColor=%23191919&shuffle=0&continuous=true"; src_url += "&onVideoDataLoaded=HPTrack.Vid.DL&onTimeUpdate=HPTrack.Vid.TC"; if (typeof(commercial_video) == "object") { src_url += "&siteSection="+commercial_video.site_and_category; if (commercial_video.package) { src_url += "&sponsorship="+commercial_video.package;  } } document.write('<scr' + 'ipt type="text/javascript" src="'+src_url+'"></scr' + 'ipt>');</script>

                                	<br />
                                </p>
		                				                            <div style="padding-left:80px;">
		                        
																By EarthTechling's Paul Willis: It could end up being about the most ambitious reverse park youve ever seen. A driver of a Nissan Leaf is...                                </div>
	                			<div class="clear">
	                			</div>
                            </div>
                    </div>

<br />
It'd be nice if the larger vehicles could be rented for reasonable prices, for when you want to take the family on a big road trip or when you want to rent a truck for hauling. (The gas savings from having a smaller vehicle would mean one should be able to afford a rental, every now and then.)			</div>

				Electric cars will eventually have self-recharging systems and in the future can become power plants when suitably parked. Selling electricity to local utilities and perhaps paying for themselves.<br />
<br />
See Moving Beyond Oil and Cheap Green at <a href="http://www.aesopinstitute.org" target="_blank" rel="nofollow">www.aesopinstitute.org</a> for a few examples of such systems under development.<br />
<br />
How soon? If there is abundant adventure capital, much more rapidly than might be imagined.<br />
<br />
If the best such Black Swans - highly improbable innovations with huge implications - had sufficient capital to accelerate development, gasoline and oil might be replaced by electric power faster than skeptics will believe possible.			</div>

				I'm with you in supporting electric vehicles, but coal plants are only about 35% efficient.  I think the real benefit comes when using renewables, such as having solar on your roof for charging. 					10:27 AM on 01/20/2013				</div>

																												
				Just one-third of the households only have a single car.  Google "number of vehicles per household".<br />
<br />
Most people (2/3) own or have access to more than one car.  Therefore an EV is definitely practical for the majority of people.  Use the EV for the bulk of daily driving (commuting, shopping etc) and get the benefit of driving at 1/5 the cost of gasoline.  Use the gas vehicle for longer trips.			</div>

		<div id="comment_222070954" class="comment_item published_comment " style="margin-left: 0px; display:block" >
						<div class="comment_top">
				
				<div class="comment_top_inner clearfix">

					<div class="author_name ">

						<div class="bio_teaser clearfix">

						<div class="author_fans">

			<div class="comment_body">
				<div class="comment_time">
					02:54 PM on 01/15/2013				</div>

																												
				Changing the price won't helpNissan needs to change both their technology and their attitude.<br />
<br />
The 2013 does not make substantive changes to the problems Nissan's version of EV technology has with both cold and hot weather.<br />
<br />
I drive a 2012 Leaf. In Chicago. Where, unlike California, we have seasons. My Leaf CANNOT HANDLE even this mild winter.<br />
<br />
I get 36 miles to a charge, on average. That's a third of the EPA rating, for those playing along at home. The car loses power when it is parked outside, which makes predicting when I need to hit a charging station something of a challenge. (I stupidly believed the salesman who told me I could definitely drive a Leaf without a home charging station...just one of many lies he told about this car.) I cannot drive outside the city. I cannot drive to the airport. And let me tell you, the frantic searches for charging stations that actually work in 12 (with the heat off, so I stand a chance of actually getting there) are loads of fun.<br />
<br />
Nissan has inspected my car and insists that it is just fine.<br />
<br />
I have received comically bad customer service both at the corporate and dealership level (my personal favorite was three days into my lease, when Mid-City Nissan offered to rent me another car for $35/day).<br />
<br />
I remain convinced that the best way for Nissan to advance electric vehicles is to get out of the EV business.			</div>

		<div id="comment_222092740" class="comment_item published_comment " style="margin-left: 50px; display:block" >
						<div class="comment_top">
				
				<div class="comment_top_inner clearfix">

					
		  <div id="comment_icons_222092740" class="float_right">

			<div class="comment_body">
				<div class="comment_time">
					03:57 PM on 01/15/2013				</div>

																												
				You CAN own a leaf without installing a home charging station, but you MUST be able to plug it in at home.  I charge my Leaf using only the Trickle charger at home, and it works fine (but there's no way I could do it if I lived in an apartment, or had to park it overnight without a place to plug it in).<br />
<br />
Also, I have found that even in our relatively mild winters here in Austin (high of 37F today), that using the heater decreases the mileage drastically.  The heat doesn't cause me much problems (for whatever reason, the AC seems to be much more efficient than the heater).<br />
<br />
For my daily commute during the winter, I pre-heat my Leaf before getting into it, and then don't run the heater while driving it.  If I run the heater, it's hard to make my round trip of ~40miles (mostly high speed highway, 65 or 70 MPH speed limits).  If I don't run the heater, I can easily get 60-70 miles range on the exact same commute.  When I first got the Leaf, I could go much farther..I made it 72 miles on the 65MPH highway with the AC, and still had 16 miles range left...I've lost one block of battery capacity after 18 months, and my range has dropped by ~15 miles).<br />
<br />
But, yeah, in general, it sounds like your Nissan dealer isn't treating you very well.  I've been very happy with mine.			</div>

				I'm glad to hear that your experience has been so much better! I really do want EVs to succeed, despite the last six months and all of this nonsense.<br />
<br />
Like a lot of urban drivers, I park in an apartment building's commercial garage overnight, and they won't let me plug in the trickle charger. (I've asked; we tried it, and I blew fuses over and over again because of the way our garage is wired.)<br />
<br />
The salesman at Mid-City knew my parking situation and said that I would be just fine relying on the commercial chargers near my office. As it turns out, no. (He claimedrepeatedlyto be the dealership's Leaf expert, and no one disagreed with him. Their real expert was on vacation. He told me, among other things, that the Leaf has a super-duper spare tire that'd get me 100 miles. The Leaf, as I'm sure you know, doesn't actually have a spare.) <br />
<br />
I don't use the heater muchusually it's actually on a/c, and I still get 3 miles per bar of battery charge. I wish the car just had a simple fan mode! And if I could plug it in, I would absolutely pre-heat it, because blowing cold air is kind of adding insult to injury when it's 12 outside.			</div>

                    });
                    var CommentsFavoriteSharer = new CommentsSharerClass({
                            type: 'vertical',
                            triggersClassName: 'share_favorite_comment_popup_trigger'
                    });
                    CommentsSharer.addPopupTriggers();
                    CommentsFavoriteSharer.addPopupTriggers();
            });

		</script>

<!-- Sailthru Horizon 'Detroit'--> 
<script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        function loadHorizon() { 
            var s = document.createElement('script'); 
            s.type = 'text/javascript'; 
            s.async = true;
            s.src = location.protocol + '//ak.sail-horizon.com/horizon/v1.js';
            var x = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; 
            x.parentNode.insertBefore(s, x);
        }
        loadHorizon();
        var oldOnLoad = window.onload;
        window.onload = function() {

            var vertical_name = 'Detroit';
            var vertical_color = HPConfig.current_vertical_color;

            if (typeof oldOnLoad === 'function') {
                oldOnLoad();
            }
            Sailthru.setup({
                domain: 'horizon.huffingtonpost.com',
                            concierge: {
                    from: 'top',
                    threshold: jQuery('.email-alert-sbm'),
                    cssPath: 'http://' + HPConfig.hp_static_domain + '/assets/css.php?f=sailthru_concierge.css&v=v1',
                    offsetBottom: 10,
                    filter: { tags: vertical_name }
                }
                        });

                    var style_modification = setInterval(function(){

                var recommendation = jQuery('.recommendation');
                if ( recommendation.length > 0 ) {

                    //removing 'HuffPost' from vertical name
                    vertical_name = jQuery.trim(vertical_name.replace(/huffpost/i, ''));
                
                    //changing style to vertical default
                    recommendation.css('border-top-color', vertical_color);
                    jQuery('.recommendationCategory').html('More in ' + vertical_name);
                    jQuery('.recommendationTitle a').css('color', vertical_color);
                    jQuery('.recommendationFooter').css('display', 'none');

                    var img = jQuery('.recommendationThumb img');

                    //if there's no image -> alternative layout
                    var alt_layout = ( img.size() == 0 );

                    //if image smaller size -> alternative layout
                    if( !alt_layout ) {

                        alt_layout = ( img[0].naturalWidth < img.width() 
                                    || img[0].naturalHeight < img.height() ); 
                             
                    }

                    if ( alt_layout ) {
                        jQuery('.recommendationThumb').css('display', 'none');
                        jQuery('.recommendationDetails').css('width', '100%');
                    }

                    //adding tracking parameters
                    jQuery('#sailthru-concierge').attr('data-beacon', '{"p":{"mnid":"sailthru_rec"}}');
                    jQuery('a.openRecommendation').attr('data-beacon','{"p":{"lnid":"open_flyout"}}');
                    jQuery('a.closeRecommendation').attr('data-beacon','{"p":{"lnid":"close_flyout"}}');
                    
                    //adding 'bN class to fire click() event
                    jQuery('.recommendationThumb a, .recommendationDetails a').addClass('bN');
              
                    clearInterval(style_modification);
                }
            }, 500);
            
            //once the flyout is shown -> send ping()
            var ping = setInterval( function() {
                
                if ( jQuery('.recommendation').css('display') == 'block' ) { 
                    bN.ping('sailthru_concierge');
                    clearInterval(ping);
                }

            }, 500);
                };
    })();
</script>
